4077  const char* limit )
4078  {

4085  goto NotFound;
4086

4089  p += 2;
4090 
4091  min = 0;
4092  max = count;
4093 
4094  while ( min < max )
4095  {
4096  int mid = ( min + max ) >> 1;
4097  const unsigned char* q = p + mid * 2;
4098  int c2;

4101  q = ft_adobe_glyph_list + ( ( (int)q[0] << 8 ) | q[1] );
4102 
4103  c2 = q[0] & 127;
4104  if ( c2 == c )
4105  {
4106  p = q;

4108  }
4109  if ( c2 < c )
4110  min = mid + 1;
4111  else

4113  }
4114  goto NotFound;
4115 
4116  Found:
4117  for (;;)
